<div id="review_2804810240" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2804810240" />
    <a title="Stella " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/86467861-stella"><img alt="Stella " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1538067157p2/86467861.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2804810240?book_show_action=true">Apr 30, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Stella " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Stella " href="/user/show/86467861-stella">Stella </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2804810240" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15587733703751046142"><br/>The title is saying how you are going to read about a book series called the mortal instruments. Obvious because it has a list of other books in the series on the back. So you ask, should I keep reading on to the rest of the series. If you are into romance, annoying boys who blame themselves for everything, and girls who just AREN’T PARTICULARLY INDEPENDENT. I mean, yes, Clary is an AWESOME character. But all she wants is to be with this annoying dude who like, LOVES THE CRAP out of her, but is </span>
  <span id="freeText15587733703751046142" style="display:none"><br />The title is saying how you are going to read about a book series called the mortal instruments. Obvious because it has a list of other books in the series on the back. So you ask, should I keep reading on to the rest of the series. If you are into romance, annoying boys who blame themselves for everything, and girls who just AREN’T PARTICULARLY INDEPENDENT. I mean, yes, Clary is an AWESOME character. But all she wants is to be with this annoying dude who like, LOVES THE CRAP out of her, but is just like, I dunno, not the boy you want this AMAZING character to end up with. You know, also, Jace just seems to always want to get something out of everything he does. AND he’s irritable. And rude. And kinda, well, RACIST. Not in a particular way, just he’s all of a sudden nice to Simon because he is suddenly in his world because, one he gets turned into ( well, I’ll let you read the book and find out) and before he was turned, he was a normal everyday human, who didn’t have all this mumbo jumbo about being in this higher race (social crud) and was just like every other normal human being and Jace was rude to him because he wasn’t his race. I mean, that’s kinda, well. RACIST. Also, the book is SO well written, but it’s that kind of book, that if you want to read it, you have to read all the gross (SEX) parts, because otherwise, you don’t know what is going on. And for all the kids out there, you know you want to skip over those parts. She’s a great writer, but there’s a lot of cursing and gross stuff for the younger audience that just want adventure. She’s also GREAT at describing stuff, and it’s honestly a book I totally recommend. But if your older than 10, DON’T RISK IT. You’ll probably be infinitely grossed the heck out. I feel like I can relate to Simon though, he’s not a total LOVER BOY like JACE. (UGH EWWWWWWWW). And he actually has some life problems. <br />If you read this book, my opinion is the cons are: Jace, he’s just infinitely annoying, Clary, she is just too reliant on a boy, it’s not a great way to show other girls what to look up to, and Sebastian, calling people VERY suggestive names (b word, c word, etc.) The pros are on the other hand: Clary, how she’s just SO AWESOME AS A PERSON! Isabelle, total amazon warrior, my favorite character, and a super cool gal. Alec, total super cool dude, a perfect example of knowing who you are, and just such an awesome fighter! Simon, super cute, but not cocky (like someone we know) supportive of Clary, and just a relatable person, because he gives everyone a person to look up to, and he’s got some problems but handles them well. Valentine, because we all need a villain. And Jocelyn, Luke, Maia, Jordan, Magnus, The wolf pack, and all the better characters you’ll notice in this book. So, if you want an awesome book, (with the exception of at least 85 gross scenes, total exaggeration, but still true to a point,) an annoying boy, and some suggestive language, you’ve got yourself a great book. <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="15587733703751046142" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_2202439110" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2202439110" />
    <a title="Jac" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/72607715-jac"><img alt="Jac" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1511406946p2/72607715.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2202439110?book_show_action=true">Dec 02, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jac" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jac" href="/user/show/72607715-jac">Jac</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/72607715-jac?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/72607715-jac?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/72607715-jac?shelf=mystery">mystery</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/72607715-jac?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2202439110" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4908825417781438235">2.5 for half loved, half hated. I enjoyed the series even though there was so much wrong with it. Some books moved a bit slowly and the angsty relationships definitely started to become the, annoying, focus as the story progressed. There were a LOT of perspectives by book 6. So much so that the scenes chopped and changed too quickly for me to really get involved with anyone on a deeper level because, by the time I got comfortable in the scene, it snapped to someone on the other side of the world</span>
  <span id="freeText4908825417781438235" style="display:none">2.5 for half loved, half hated. I enjoyed the series even though there was so much wrong with it. Some books moved a bit slowly and the angsty relationships definitely started to become the, annoying, focus as the story progressed. There were a LOT of perspectives by book 6. So much so that the scenes chopped and changed too quickly for me to really get involved with anyone on a deeper level because, by the time I got comfortable in the scene, it snapped to someone on the other side of the world. I started to disconnect from the main characters after a while because so many of the bit-characters started getting their own scenes thrown in left right and centre. The worst part was that many of these characters added little to the plot, they felt like they were there to simply fill pages or try grab readers for the spin-off series.<br /><br />The story was different with an interesting take on the idea of demons and neph angels and I couldn’t ever guess at where the story was heading. I liked Sebastian and my heart broke for him. It was fun to see and antagonist as a central character, to see him be a part of the main characters lives and I thought he was as developed as the others. His journey was an enjoyable read and I was pro his agender because he wasn’t whiny and relationship focused like so many of the ‘heroes.’<br /><br />I couldn’t really get into the relationships as much as I would have liked. To me, Isabelle and Simon were a weird, awkward to read, combo that felt pushed together, like the author couldn’t have any happily single characters by the end; like, how sad would that be if some of the strong, independent character ended up strong and independent? I also felt my pro 'Clary and Jace' wavered the more the series progressed and they finally lost me when <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ they had sex in the demon world. Really? Really!! Was it because they finally could now that Jace had lost his burny angel fire? Get it done as soon as possible? Super romantic after a five book build up. Really location and situation appropriate. Also, who purposely brings their wallet and condom stash to a demon world??  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> <br /><br />Overall there was great world-building (plagiarism aside), the series was well written for the most part and the story was easy enough to follow, if you pushed aside all the fluff to focus to find it, with enough twists and turns to keep you hooked and engaged.</span>
  <a data-text-id="4908825417781438235" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer6092667083743413821">"The Mortal Instruments starts off at the pandemonium club with Clary and Simon visiting it. Though they are unaware of it that PanDEMONium club is a place where downworlders and demons lurk with humans (mundanes). Thus begins a saga that unfolds truths of Clary's past. The ugly characters which were well forgotten in history are coming back. Clary, with Simon, Jace, Alec and Isabelle has to fight all odds and also a war (or two) to reach the ultimate truth. But in this process, will she lose he</span>
  <span id="freeText6092667083743413821" style="display:none">"The Mortal Instruments starts off at the pandemonium club with Clary and Simon visiting it. Though they are unaware of it that PanDEMONium club is a place where downworlders and demons lurk with humans (mundanes). Thus begins a saga that unfolds truths of Clary's past. The ugly characters which were well forgotten in history are coming back. Clary, with Simon, Jace, Alec and Isabelle has to fight all odds and also a war (or two) to reach the ultimate truth. But in this process, will she lose herself, or find a new self which she never knew about?"<br /><br />I don't know how did I survive without this book series for such a long time man! The Mortal Instruments is something i personally will recommend you all to read. It's the best YA fiction out there. The Romance, the rich world, the characters, the storytelling and the plot is not conventional, its something way out of the ordinary and way ahead of its times. The world of shadowhunters is so simple yet there is so much intricacy the author has put while weaving it!<br /><br />There are vampires, werewolves, faeries, warlocks, ir must I say, hot warlocks *winks*. I seriously am in love with all the relationships portrayed in the book. It's all so authentic, so original and so organic. I didnt find anything that is not good enough or not upto the mark in the series. Also, TMI is a series that you will never get bored of. You can read it and then start it again and then again and you'll want more because everytime you read, you discover new things you didnt notice the last time you read it.<br /><br />Thankyou!🙌</span>

  <span id="freeText10568358702522891737" style="display:none">I never thought I'll be a fan of this series, being a HP and Rick Riordan fan. I fell in love with this book immediately.<br /><br />All these characters, stay in heart forever.<br /><br />A short review of all the characters.. Jace.. He has all qualities that make a girl fall in love with him.. handsome, courageous, and ready to die for friends.. And the way he expresses his love for Clary, made me really jealous of her.<br /><br />Next is Clary.. in the first trilogy, i didn't like her.. But she quickly learnt the ways of shadow hunters.. and became heroic.. and adorable..<br /><br />Simon.. the poor soul in the series.. who was dragged into the shadow hunter's world, and always has a broken heart.. and he is one of the best persons to have as a Friend.. <br /><br />Then Alex , Isabelle and Magnus.. all have their own uniqueness..<br /><br />And not to mention, Sebastian.. at the end of the 1st trilogy, i hated him, and believed that he deserved to die.. but after the climax of the book, i felt really sorry for him..<br /><br />He is the brother, Clary can never have.. it touched me.. if and only if, his father didn't give him the devil's blood, he would have been A great shadow hunter..<br /><br />Overall, it's a wonderful book to read..</span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3496644111" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1859836585539658444">I can see why some people might find this series unappealing, but honestly I kind of love it! The protagonist Clare is sarcastic, caring and has a good development throughout the series; the romantic relationship between Jace and her is cute and while there are some controversial and/or doubting instances such as the weird pseudo-incest and the angst and melodrama (especially on book 4, which is my least favorite), I think there's room to see how they ended caring for each other, why they got at</span>
  <span id="freeText1859836585539658444" style="display:none">I can see why some people might find this series unappealing, but honestly I kind of love it! The protagonist Clare is sarcastic, caring and has a good development throughout the series; the romantic relationship between Jace and her is cute and while there are some controversial and/or doubting instances such as the weird pseudo-incest and the angst and melodrama (especially on book 4, which is my least favorite), I think there's room to see how they ended caring for each other, why they got attracted to each other as well as how their interactions and banters developed; and of course, the interactions among all the characters is great! And by the end of book 6 you see how they become a family. I would not recommend this to anyone and I definitely cannot argue this saga is good in anyway, but I honestly have fun and for know I will stick until the end of the Shadowhunters Chronicles. <br /><br />(And of course, Malec is wholesome... Aaand Magnus Bane is one of the best characters I ever read, and Cassandra Clare knows it, since he seems to be in all iterations of the Shadowhunters).</span>

          </span>

      <div class="reviewFooter uitext buttons">

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2921571000" />
    <a title="Leslie Bates" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/99890138-leslie-bates"><img alt="Leslie Bates" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1598731088p2/99890138.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2921571000?book_show_action=true">Aug 02, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Leslie Bates" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Leslie Bates" href="/user/show/99890138-leslie-bates">Leslie Bates</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2921571000" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11924159025540128574">For those who are captivated by a different world where the unimaginable is real. Angels and demons, vampires and werewolves, warlocks and faeries. All these exist. Where no one is just ordinary, but extraordinary. A series based off the works of books like Dante's Inferno and Paradise Lost, with a twist and references to angels and demons like Lilith and Lucifer who reign over hell. A fantastic read that will keep the reader turning the pages not wanting to put the book down. You will fall in l</span>
  <span id="freeText11924159025540128574" style="display:none">For those who are captivated by a different world where the unimaginable is real. Angels and demons, vampires and werewolves, warlocks and faeries. All these exist. Where no one is just ordinary, but extraordinary. A series based off the works of books like Dante's Inferno and Paradise Lost, with a twist and references to angels and demons like Lilith and Lucifer who reign over hell. A fantastic read that will keep the reader turning the pages not wanting to put the book down. You will fall in love with the characters, and see yourself relating to pretty much each one. A book that blurs the line of being a good person and doing evil things, sacrifices, love and betrayals, friendship and family and becoming the person you are meant to me. I highly suggest those who want to get lost in the world of Shawdowhunters read the series and then if you want, watch the TV Show, Shadowhunters. Both will not disappoint you. </span>
  <a data-text-id="11924159025540128574" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer2605806399804643510">A World filled with Magic, Vampires, Demons, Angels, Werewolfs...and many more...but a new magical creatures which are called "Shadowhunters". Cassandra Clare is an amazing author who writes with care and passion and presents exciting plots and unforgettable characters. The villian Sebastian Morgenstern is one of the most intriguing characters i have ever come to read about, and Jace Wayland (dreamy sigh) are one of my favourite book-boyfriend ever. I adore his arrogance, wild-ness, bravery, wit</span>
  <span id="freeText2605806399804643510" style="display:none">A World filled with Magic, Vampires, Demons, Angels, Werewolfs...and many more...but a new magical creatures which are called "Shadowhunters". Cassandra Clare is an amazing author who writes with care and passion and presents exciting plots and unforgettable characters. The villian Sebastian Morgenstern is one of the most intriguing characters i have ever come to read about, and Jace Wayland (dreamy sigh) are one of my favourite book-boyfriend ever. I adore his arrogance, wild-ness, bravery, wit, cocky comebacks, charm and ultimate devotion and love for his soulmate, the main-heroine Clary Fray. All six books in this series are filled amazing 5-STARS, but my true favourite which stole my whole heart has to be the third book "City of Glass". "The Mortal Instruments"-series made me hold my breath of excitement, laugh my ass off and cry both sad and happy tears.!</span>

    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3237329824?book_show_action=true">Mar 19, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Shira G" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Shira G" href="/user/show/100338581-shira-g">Shira G</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <a class="lightGreyText" title=" " href="/book/show/24270249-the-mortal-instruments-box-set">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3237329824" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9732216383831646070">These books have kept me up until midnight trying to finish on school nights, had me forgetting homework and meals, and had me so intrigued I finished them all in about a month. I love the main character and how she explores this new world around her as a teenager. I love the authors amazing descriptions and how she puts so much feeling into everyone and every aspect of the book. This book is such a page turner that once you get into the world you can't get out. As a young adult dystopian and fa</span>
  <span id="freeText9732216383831646070" style="display:none">These books have kept me up until midnight trying to finish on school nights, had me forgetting homework and meals, and had me so intrigued I finished them all in about a month. I love the main character and how she explores this new world around her as a teenager. I love the authors amazing descriptions and how she puts so much feeling into everyone and every aspect of the book. This book is such a page turner that once you get into the world you can't get out. As a young adult dystopian and fantasy reader, I figured this would just be another stereotypical novel with the same plot as the main character rebelling against her world, but this was far from it. I highly recommend these books to anyone who is interested in this genre. Love these books!</span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Saffron Mavros" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Saffron Mavros" href="/user/show/13004295-saffron-mavros">Saffron Mavros</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3416995083" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10656077205866602751">Even though it's a long series and some parts are drab and stretched beyond their premises, the plot and the storyline are extra-ordinary and mind-blowing. <br/><br/>At no point, does it get boring. Every chapter adds new information to the building crescendo until all of it boils down together in the final book, creating an impetuous rhythm that takes off in the final few chapters, pulling everything together and bursting through the mind, igniting a flurry of senses. <br/><br/>The way all the characters are tied </span>
  <span id="freeText10656077205866602751" style="display:none">Even though it's a long series and some parts are drab and stretched beyond their premises, the plot and the storyline are extra-ordinary and mind-blowing. <br /><br />At no point, does it get boring. Every chapter adds new information to the building crescendo until all of it boils down together in the final book, creating an impetuous rhythm that takes off in the final few chapters, pulling everything together and bursting through the mind, igniting a flurry of senses. <br /><br />The way all the characters are tied together, building up to the final battle for good, honor and love, is so commendable and smooth that it doesn't even feel like it's ending. Like a beautiful closure to a story, you dedicated your precious time to. </span>
  <a data-text-id="10656077205866602751" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_3273120492" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3273120492" />
    <a title="Kirstyn" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/94178830-kirstyn"><img alt="Kirstyn" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1587372510p2/94178830.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3273120492?book_show_action=true">Apr 10, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kirstyn" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kirstyn" href="/user/show/94178830-kirstyn">Kirstyn</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3273120492" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7069551690192000092">This is a popular series and I don't get the hype. <br/> I felt that the books lost their way plot wise somewhere around the 4th book and it didn't have the best start with the whole incest thing. I had a friend tell me that when they finished this series they felt bereft, like they'd left friends behind and whilst I am familiar with this feeling I certainly didn't get it from this series. I really couldn't have cared less. The only notable character exceptions were Simon and Magnus, both of whom I l</span>
  <span id="freeText7069551690192000092" style="display:none">This is a popular series and I don't get the hype. <br /> I felt that the books lost their way plot wise somewhere around the 4th book and it didn't have the best start with the whole incest thing. I had a friend tell me that when they finished this series they felt bereft, like they'd left friends behind and whilst I am familiar with this feeling I certainly didn't get it from this series. I really couldn't have cared less. The only notable character exceptions were Simon and Magnus, both of whom I liked and enjoyed being present in scenes. I found the romance flat and two dimensional. <br />I finished the series but I wonder often why I did. Probably because I'd bought them as a set.</span>
  <a data-text-id="7069551690192000092" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('itmJyKynwTRoi/29GazK7YvSoZqHMdU2NIHLga8bFFt4i4umcRMiQse3f5Io0pAwqK27dEvB5AVtrUAfJrOOww==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('LKCv449PxsF65TE63F82/ynuzbo0kLYfCNmQrIgCozfe8q2NUvslt9XZsxXtIWwiCpHXVPhghyxR9RsyAao5rw==')})
  }

<span id="freeTextContainer13046168764856951126">Hello Goodreadsers. Here's my official bio:<br/><br/>"Cassandra Clare was born overseas and spent her early years traveling around the world with her family and several trunks of fantasy books. Cassandra worked for several years as an entertainment journalist for the Hollywood Reporter before turning her attention to fiction. She is the author of City of Bones, the first book in the Mortal Instruments trilo</span>
  <span id="freeText13046168764856951126" style="display:none">Hello Goodreadsers. Here's my official bio:<br /><br />"Cassandra Clare was born overseas and spent her early years traveling around the world with her family and several trunks of fantasy books. Cassandra worked for several years as an entertainment journalist for the Hollywood Reporter before turning her attention to fiction. She is the author of City of Bones, the first book in the Mortal Instruments trilogy and a New York Times bestseller. Cassandra lives with her fiance and their two cats in Massachusetts."<br /><br />You can find me online at <br /><br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.cassandraclare.com">www.cassandraclare.com</a><br /><br />I have a blog:<br /><br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://cassandraclare.livejournal.com/">http://cassandraclare.livejournal.com/</a><br /><br />and a Facebook:<br /><br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.facebook.com/Cassandraclare">http://www.facebook.com/Cassandraclare</a><br /><br />and a Twitter:<br /><br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.twitter.com/cassieclare">www.twitter.com/cassieclare</a><br /><br />I'll be available here on Goodreads to answer questions for a Goodreads Author Discussion starting September 18 — <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.goodreads.com/group/show/37113.Q_A_with_Cassandra_Clare">http://www.goodreads.com/group/show/3...</a><br /><br />Go sign up so you don't miss the conversation when it starts!</span>
